2 Name: lolocaust!rsvcwx6Axc 2005-04-04 15:56 ID:Heaven

Giko's favorite phrase is "ITTEYOSHI!!"

　　＿＿__＿∧∧　　 ／￣￣￣￣￣￣￣
～'　＿＿__（　ﾟДﾟ）＜　　逝ってよし！！
　 ＵU 　 　Ｕ U　　　 ＼＿＿＿＿＿＿＿

This often gets translated as with "Go and die" or "Kill yourself" or "Fuck off". All of these translations seem to be not getting the jist of the expression, though, since "Itteyoshi" is a play on words: http://4-ch.net/nihongo/kareha.pl/1101446156/55

    > If you're a japanese and hear it without seeing the chinese character used in it,
    > then you will think it means "you may go" ,or "go away" in a less dominant imperative.
    > But if you read it while seeing the chinese character,
    > it means "you may kill yourself" or "kill yourself".
    >
    > You can use this phrase when someone posts a silly remark or
    > asserts something with lame evidence.
    >
    > note: "行く(iku)" means "to go", "逝く(iku)" means "to die".

3 Name: lolocaust!rsvcwx6Axc 2005-04-04 16:06 ID:Heaven

　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　＼　│　／
　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　／￣＼　　 ／￣￣￣￣￣￣￣￣￣
　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　─（ ﾟ ∀ ﾟ ）＜　SAITAMASAITAMA！
　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　＼＿／　　 ＼＿＿＿＿＿＿＿＿＿
　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　／　│　＼
　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　 ∩ ∧　∧　　／￣￣￣￣￣￣￣￣￣￣
￣￣￣￣￣￣￣￣＼∩ ∧　∧　＼（ ﾟ∀ﾟ）＜ SaitamaSaitamaSaitama！
Saitamaaaaaaa！ 　 ＞（ ﾟ∀ﾟ ）/ ｜　　　　/　＼＿＿＿＿＿＿＿＿＿＿
＿＿＿＿＿＿＿＿／ ｜　　　 〈　｜　　　｜
　　　　　　　　　　　　　 /　／＼_」　/　／＼」
　　　　　　　　　　　　　 ￣　　　　 / ／

Originates from a logo of the Liberal Democratic Party of Japan:

http://web.archive.org/web/20021018125339/http://www.jimin.jp/jimin/jimin/t_rogo.html

Soon after this logo became known, AA were created for the "Liberal-Democratic Monar Party"

There are various theories as to why the characters have begun shouting SAITAMA without an end:
http://members.at.infoseek.co.jp/maruheso/aadic/sa.html#saitama

But as Saitama, a prefecture in Japan (and also the name of its capital city), is known for funny news coming from it, the enthusiasm expressed by these cute little fellas can easily be understood.

KUMA ("Bear") is a natural kind of guy. He likes to frollick through town and chase after some pretty girls (some evil folk dubbed him "Pedobear" for that). He doesn't want to work and just enjoy himself. So he's a pretty cool dude. But sometimes he has to defeat himself rather roughly whenever his arch rival, Ronald McDonald, tries to get in on his act again by destroying his beloved environment or other evil schemes. 16 Name: CTRL+C & CTRL+V 2005-04-07 14:44 ID:Heaven

NIDA

Nida is a Korean, and as such his prominent features are funny shoes, high cheek bones and a disingenuous personality.
Most of the time he can be seen spreading filthy lies about alleged Japanese war crimes or simply grouping together with other Nidas in order to start up some mischief.
His favorite drink is apology juice (a joke based on an actual photo of some Korean politicians protesting, one of them holding a sign which was supposed to read "I demand an apology" but was misspelled and thus read "Apology Juice")
　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　
　　　∧＿∧　
　　 <丶｀∀´>　　I DEMAND APOLOGY AND COMPENSATION NIDA!
　　 （　　　　）　
　　 ｜ ｜　|　　　
　　 〈＿フ__フ.

天皇陛下の前立腺の中の人
("The person in the Emperor's Prostate"?)

Mysterious AA charcter which appears suddenly, saying "I am sorry, just passing through ..."
There isn't a common name decided, yet. There is also rumor that he is the soul that wanders within 2channel. (Seemingly, it is never in a bad mood)
Although he is always walking, he may sit down occasionally and sometimes stay for a long time.

"Chinesemen are members of the Hominoidea superfamily of primates
and also belongs to the human race"

should it live?
should it die?
that is not a problem at all.

life, death, tanasinn

tanasinn=occult,cult,fascism,death,life,relision・・・,or・・・?

tanasinn operates the whole world.
tanasinn is the soul of the universe.
tanasinn is the bottom of your heart.
tanasinn transcends surrealism and realism.
tanasinn is inherent in every self.
tanasinn is inherent in every structure.
tanasinn is inherent in every system.
tanasinn is decadent and may cause self-collapse.

tanasinn vacumeir alles
tanasinn plays with all elements

The Messenger of fear
The Child of darkness and confusion
The King of infinite decomposition
The Khaos

tanasinn

tanasinn absodivides the WORLD

Words cannot explain tanasinn. More accurate:
Don't think. Feel and you'll be tanasinn.

full-length mirror Evening glow Wave of those passing
Disappear wholly. Roadside tree murmured in the heart Swing
with a child which tries to be the first Scene

fall with you and it falls

The Sasuga Brothers (流石兄弟)

　　　　　　　　　　　 ∧＿∧
　　　　　∧＿∧ 　（´<_｀ 　） I see what you did there.
　　　　 （　´_ゝ`）　/　　 ⌒i
　　　　／　　　＼　 　　　|　|

　 ＿_(__ﾆつ/　 FMV　 / .| .|＿＿＿＿
　 　　　 ＼/＿＿＿＿/　（u　⊃


The elder brother (the left one, sitting on the PC, his name is Anisha) likes to watch guro,
porn and other naughty stuff.
He is kind of stupid and often falls for browser crashing sites.
The younger brother's name is Otoutosha (Anisha & Otoutosha translate to "older brother"
and "younger brother"). He likes to make fun of his elder brother.

They often both do a kind of masochistic tsukkomi act which is difficult to translate.
(http://www.japannewbie.com/archives/000122.html)

I don't quite know how to translate their favorite phrase (流石, it also appears in their name) -
it could mean something along the lines of "saw that one coming" or "indeed" or "clever".
Maybe someone with a bit more knowledge of Japanese can help us out here.

>>53

（　´_ゝ`）ﾌｰﾝ

Fuun-face is used for expressing a feeling of being indifferent. English equivalent of the word fuun would be "okay, so what?". Fuun is a character personified from this face-mark.

レモナ 【れもな】
女性（？）キャラの一つ。最初はネカマキャラとして構想されたらしい。
男女同体とかいう説もある。モナーを恋い慕っている。

＊裏設定：実はモナ研で作られた生体兵器でもあり、恐るべき破壊能力を持つ。
　バイオ技術で各種細胞を合成して生まれたが、そのとき、交通事故で氏んだモナーの恋人の
　脳細胞も利用。生前の記憶は無いが、モナーを恋い慕って居候しに来たらしい。
　たまに生前の記憶が復活することもある。

78 Name: Shika Shaker 2005-05-25 16:48 ID:Heaven

"Sasuga" is difficult to translate on its own, but "sasuga sam" is a mix of the english "that's our sam" and "i knew sam could do it!" Essentially both the predictability of what happened is being emphasized, but it carries connotations of praise.

81 Name: CTRL+C & CTRL+V 2005-06-08 16:16 ID:Heaven

Often confused by Westerners: Monar and Moralar

MONAR


　　 ∧＿∧　　／￣￣￣￣￣￣￣￣
　　（　´∀｀）＜　Look who's talking
　　（　　　　） 　＼＿＿＿＿＿＿＿＿
　　｜ ｜　|
　　（_＿）＿）

http://members.at.infoseek.co.jp/maruheso/aadic/ma.html#mona-

The most famous character of 2channel!
Main appearance is in reference to another post which seems to be hypocritical.
Monar then says "OMAEMONA" which roughly translates to "you, too" but is better
translated in the version used above.
A large variety of derivation characters have been invented ever since Monar came up and the influence on today's 2channel AA is inscrutable.

(I have given up on making sense of the rest of the character origin legend.
Monar seems to have been invented on 2channels "Kitchen" board (where you invent, test and generally play around with kopipe material), but that's all I am getting from it.)


MORALAR

　 ∧＿∧ 　　／￣￣￣￣￣￣￣
　（　・∀・）＜　mataｰRISIYOUYO♪
　（　　　　） 　＼＿＿＿＿＿＿＿
　｜ ｜　|
　（_＿）＿）


http://members.at.infoseek.co.jp/maruheso/aadic/ma.html#morara


A character that debuted as the "Conscience of two channels" in April, 2000 to cross morality with Monar.

It was hardly used for a conscientious remark though it was being widely used as a surreal gag, a
slaughter, and a homosexual hentai character as of now.
Moreover, "Stop it" as a usual habit of saying when appearing is hardly being used now.
"Secus" and "Matarri", etc. inspired by the Morarar tone have spread in 2channel and the whole land of the net.

(I have no idea how to translate "Matarri", etc. so I left them as they were)

Hitahita (ヒタヒタ)
Derived from the AA of the guy in >>23, also hangs out with him.
He might be some kind of seal but then again he might not!
His name comes from the sound he makes by tiptoeing around quickly.

Hikky is one of the oldest AA characters from 2ch and even predates Monar.
Originally he was just supposed to be a depressed orphan named "Masao Komori"
(the picture behind him is of deceased father).
He thinks about things in a very negative way, takes a pessimistic point of view
and mostly hangs his head. Over the time he was more and more used to represent
the prototypical withdrawn youth of contemporary Japan's society, the hikikomori:
http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hikikomori

http://maruheso.at.infoseek.co.jp/aadic/ha.html#hikky


Sites that collect Hikky AA & other stuff:

http://members.at.infoseek.co.jp/ktttm/
http://www.wcn.to/~gappa/hikky/

Dokuo (毒男)
AA to express lonely, single men.
He always thinks of everybody and everything else as rotten & disgusting.
Typically, he is represented in the above manner,
with creaking and moaning sounds coming from the next appartment.
He has a tendency to develop mental problems and kill himself in the end.

He originated on the 2channel board for single men.

http://maruheso.at.infoseek.co.jp/aadic/ta.html#dokuo

Shii (しぃ) is female and cute. At some point she was abandoned and now she lives in a cardboard box. She is Giko's girlfriend. It's unclear whether her name is supposed to mean "C", "ayashii" (strange), or "she". Other characters (especially Moraler) like to hate on Shii a lot.

Giko Cat (ギコ猫)

- A pretty hateful little cat that likes to spout abusive, vulgar and offensive language and does not concern himself with flattering people.
- His most popular catchphrases are "GO & DIE!"(untranslatable, see >>2) "snarl" and "gikohahaha" (the latter being some phrase already used in 1994, before the AA)
- Has a habit of talking in first person (huge ego)
- First reported sighting in 1999, before 2channel.
- He's been established as Shii's boyfriend.

There are various rumors and mysteries about Giko cat, his origin and his behaviour.
Lots of new characters were modeled after him and he is likely the second most popular AA character on 2channel after Mona.

http://maruheso.at.infoseek.co.jp/aadic/ka.html#gikoneko

BIGURU。(る)名前としてのモチーフとしてBIGURU犬を使用したのはASCII芸術KYARAです――
「ペットの犬に中へ、どれ、氏、遠方に渡された第1のBIGURUSUREのうちの1――それは
そうです、何、Taro氏」モデルBIGURU--美しい外観--であ??a作用するという立場、謙遜--
謙遜および礼儀――セット・アップ、正しい特徴「そしてぞぬとしぃ"の関係などのよい
支持者――私の2つつごとのMONAボード--それは、したがって、多くのよいASCII芸術を
生産し、かつBIGURUに同時に魅力の目標にさせるために来ました、付着質な荒らし――
頑強な叩きの仕事およびイメージは落ちます、それまで実行される、今日の終了までに
結果、しかしながら(そのような多数の賢い試みに関係なく)BIGURU――まだ(さらに)
思慮深いMONA、居住者および職人--たち--を板で囲う、最も大きな支援を集めることは
「BIGURU」のASCII芸術としての完全の。
165 Name: I am 日本人 2005-11-28 08:14 ID:CKhVU/6E

poopoo　means UNKO??
166 Name: Yes. 2005-12-07 05:00 ID:/XNjrocc

>>165
There are many English words that mean "unko." "poopoo" or "poo" or "poop" or "poopy" is the way a small child might say it and it is used for humorous effect here. More commonly are other words, more vulgar, like "shit" or "crap." A doctor would say "stool" or "feces" in a medical context.

175 Name: CTRL+C & CTRL+V 2006-01-20 04:12 ID:3VTMNB+o

>>171
You can cut and paste AA from pretty much any browser to Word these days, if you have the Japanese fonts installed. Paste what you want into Word, do a "select all" (Ctrl-A) and set the font to "MS PGothic". That should be all you need to do.

奇形モララー【きけいもららー】

人手不足のため分裂を試みるが失敗し１のような姿に。

181 Name: = 。= 2006-01-24 14:58 ID:Heaven

>>176
彡's sound is not a "kami" .

【彡】 [サン、セン/] san,sen/ 毛の長いさま
The pronunciation of this Kanji character is a San or Sen.
The meaning shows the appearance with a long hair.
I do not think that it records in the dictionary in PC because
it cannot convert it by"san" nor"sen".
There are many Kanji characters that cannot be converted with PC
though it can be seen in s-jJIS AA..

【冫】 [ヒョウ/] hyou/ 氷(ice)
【勹】 [ホウ/] hou/ 包む(wrap)
【卩】 [セツ、セチ/] setsu,sechi/ふし(節=knot)
【亠】 [トウ/] tou/なべぶた(部首の名＝a part of Kanji)
【匕】 [ヒ/] hi/ さじ(匙＝spoon) *a little different from 七(seven)
【乂】 [ガイ/] gai くさぎる(草を刈る=cut the grass)、治める(govern)
http://www.kanjiworld.com/kanji.php?start=4E42&lang=uk&gr=no&les=3
【儿】 [ジン、ニン/] jin,nin/人(person)
http://www.kanjiworld.com/kanji.php?start=513F&lang=&gr=&les=
【从】 [ジュウ、シュウ、ジュ/] jyu, shu, ju 従,從(=follow)
【巛】 [セン/] sen/ 川 (river)
【幺】 [ヨウ/] yo u/小さい、幼い（little,infancy)
【弋】 [ヨウ/] yo u
【殳】 [シュ、ズ/ほこ] shu,zu/hoko
【爻】 [コウ/] kou/
【爿】 [ショウ/] shou/
【夲】 [トウ、ホン/] tou,hon

361 Name: !wOTDXDxvTc : 2008-09-21 20:46 ID:BXWEuuu5

362 Name: CTRL+C & CTRL+V : 2008-09-25 18:03 ID:l7sQJIM4
>>360
Tanasinn is everything and nothing. It's not something you "get". Don't think, feel and you'll be tanasinn.

In all seriousness it's just another odd 2ch meme, stemming from a corrupted/surreal/psychedelic SJIS art of Doraemon. Imagine Salvador Dalí with Parkinson's doing SJIS.

Some people seem to take tanasinn way too seriously (ironically enough), as if it were some kind of interbutts incarnation of the Akashic records, Leary's 8th circuit of consciousness, or the Hindu Brahman ("substrate of life") concept. Om- That supreme Brahman tanasinn is infinite, and this conditioned Brahman tanasinn is infinite. The infinite proceeds from infinite. Then through knowledge, realizing the infinitude of the infinite, it remains as infinite alone.

There are many other theories as to the etymology and meaning of the term, eg: tan(a) sin(n). See tanasinn.org.

364 Name: CTRL+C & CTRL+V : 2008-09-26 09:48 ID:f1eRUg52
just curious though,

is it a bad thing to post these ASCII on places other than 4-ch.net or 2channel? Even if you acknowledge where they came from?
365 Name: CTRL+C & CTRL+V : 2008-09-26 19:42 ID:Heaven
>>364
Generally speaking, it's not a bad thing. Kopipe (copy+paste) is very prevalent on 2channel-style BBS; anyone posting original SJIS art would be very foolish to believe that their work won't be kopiped all over the place. Personally, if I created an original SJIS art (lol, fat chance) and it got kopiped a bunch, I'd feel honored.

Attribution is usually not given, most likely because anybody who's in the know will assume it's kopiped from 2channel.
366 Name: CTRL+C & CTRL+V : 2008-09-27 01:15 ID:Heaven
>>358
They're kaomoji, apparently waving their hands in the air. Kaomoji are a nifty Japanese version of emoticons. The DQN board here has names for some of the ones you've posted; although on DQN they're used a bit differently than on Japanese sites, where they're interjected into normal text like western style emoticons, as in the latter example you gave.
